短者不为不足,duan'zhe'bu'wei'bu'zu
端正而不知以为义,duan'zheng'er'bu'zhi'yi'wei'yi
断之则悲,duan'zhi'ze'bei
对曰,dui'yue
对云将曰,dui'yun'jiang'yue
蹲乎会稽,dun'hu'kuai'ji
遁其天,dun'qi'tian
蹲循勿争,dun'xun'wu'zheng
敦杖,dun'zhang
夺彼与此,duo'bi'yu'ci
多辞缪说,duo'ci'miu'shuo
掇而不岐,duo'er'bu'qi
多而无已,duo'er'wu'yi
堕尔形体,duo'er'xing'ti
多方乎仁义而用之者,duo'fang'hu'ren'yi'er'yong'zhi'zhe
多积财而不得尽用,duo'ji'cai'er'bu'de'jin'yong
多男子而授之职,duo'nan'zi'er'shou'zhi'zhi
多男子则多惧,duo'nan'zi'ze'duo'ju
多能明之,duo'neng'ming'zhi
堕其天囊,duo'qi'tian'nang
堕汝形骸,duo'ru'xing'hai
多为身弃生以殉物,duo'wei'shen'qi'sheng'yi'xun'wu
多文骈枝于五藏之情者,duo'wen'pian'zhi'yu'wu'cang'zhi'qing'zhe
多信者显,duo'xin'zhe'xian
多以裘褐为衣,duo'yi'qiu'he'wei'yi
多有似封人之所谓,duo'you'si'feng'ren'zhi'suo'wei
多于聪者,duo'yu'cong'zhe
多于之赢,duo'yu'zhi'ying
多则扰,duo'ze'rao
堕肢体,duo'zhi'ti
多知为败,duo'zhi'wei'bai
恶成不及改,e'cheng'bu'ji'gai
恶得不谓之人,e'de'bu'wei'zhi'ren
恶得无情,e'de'wu'qing
俄而有无矣,e'er'you'wu'yi
俄而子来有病,e'er'zi'lai'you'bing
俄而子舆有病,e'er'zi'yu'you'bing
恶乎不可,e'hu'bu'ke
恶乎不然,e'hu'bu'ran
恶乎介也,e'hu'jie'ye
恶乎惊,e'hu'jing
恶乎可,e'hu'ke
恶乎其所不适,e'hu'qi'suo'bu'shi
恶乎其所适,e'hu'qi'suo'shi
恶乎然,e'hu'ran
饿虎杀而食之,e'hu'sha'er'shi'zhi
恶乎往而不可哉,e'hu'wang'er'bu'ke'zai
恶乎在,e'hu'zai
恶乎至,e'hu'zhi
恶乎知君子小人哉,e'hu'zhi'jun'zi'xiao'ren'zai
恶可,e'ke
恶可而言,e'ke'er'yan
恶来死,e'lai'si
恶能正之,e'neng'zheng'zhi
恶器也,e'qi'ye
俄然觉,e'ran'jue
恶人之天,e'ren'zhi'tian
恶识所以不然,e'shi'suo'yi'bu'ran
恶识所以然,e'shi'suo'yi'ran
恶往而不暇,e'wang'er'bu'xia
恶为君之患也,e'wei'jun'zhi'huan'ye
恶用德,e'yong'de
恶用而求有以异,e'yong'er'qiu'you'yi'yi
恶用胶,e'yong'jiao
恶用商,e'yong'shang
恶用知,e'yong'zhi
恶有人灾也,e'you'ren'zai'ye
恶欲喜怒哀乐六者,e'yu'xi'nu'ai'le'liu'zhe
恶者贵而美者贱,e'zhe'gui'er'mei'zhe'jian
恶知不化哉,e'zhi'bu'hua'zai
恶至而倪贵贱,e'zhi'er'ni'gui'jian
恶至而倪小大,e'zhi'er'ni'xiao'da
恶知已化哉,e'zhi'yi'hua'zai
而哀不己若者,er'ai'bu'ji'ruo'zhe
而爱有所亡,er'ai'you'suo'wang

而百姓猖狂,er'bai'xing'chang'kuang

妄称文武,wang'cheng'wen'wu
王大悦之,wang'da'yue'zhi
王骀,wang'dai
王独不见夫腾猿乎,wang'du'bu'jian'fu'teng'yuan'hu
往而不返,wang'er'bu'fan
忘而复之,wang'er'fu'zhi
王公必将乘人而斗其捷,wang'gong'bi'jiang'cheng'ren'er'dou'qi'jie
王顾谓其友颜不疑曰,wang'gu'wei'qi'you'yan'bu'yi'yue
网罟之所布,wang'gu'zhi'suo'bu
亡国而不失人心,wang'guo'er'bu'shi'ren'xin
王果曰,wang'guo'yue
忘乎天,wang'hu'tian
忘乎物,wang'hu'wu
王季为适,wang'ji'wei'shi

王巾笥而藏之庙堂之上,wang'jin'si'er'cang'zhi'miao'tang'zhi'shang
罔两问景曰,wang'liang'wen'jing'yue
王命相者趋射之,wang'ming'xiang'zhe'qu'she'zhi
王乃牵而上殿,wang'nai'qian'er'shang'dian
王乃校剑士七日,wang'nai'xiao'jian'shi'qi'ri
王乃悦之,wang'nai'yue'zhi
王倪曰,wang'ni'yue
王倪之师曰被衣,wang'ni'zhi'shi'yue'bei'yi
忘年忘义,wang'nian'wang'yi

亡其略弗及下,wang'qi'lue'fu'ji'xia

王其无它,wang'qi'wu'ta

忘人,wang'ren
王三环之,wang'san'huan'zhi
王射之,wang'she'zhi
亡身不真,wang'shen'bu'zhen
往世不可追也,wang'shi'bu'ke'zhui'ye
忘适之适也,wang'shi'zhi'shi'ye
王使诸梁也甚重,wang'shi'zhu'liang'ye'shen'zhong

往矣,wang'yi
忘已之人,wang'yi'zhi'ren
王有所成,wang'you'suo'cheng
王与蛮氏有辩乎,wang'yu'man'shi'you'bian'hu
王予搜援绥登车,wang'yu'sou'yuan'sui'deng'che
王曰,wang'yue
妄则其信之也莫,wang'ze'qi'xin'zhi'ye'mo
往者勿止,wang'zhe'wu'zhi
望之畅然,wang'zhi'chang'ran
望之而不见其崖,wang'zhi'er'bu'jian'qi'ya
望之而不能见也,wang'zhi'er'bu'neng'jian'ye
望之久矣,wang'zhi'jiu'yi
望之似木鸡矣,wang'zhi'si'mu'ji'yi
忘之所起也,wang'zhi'suo'qi'ye
王子庆忌见而问焉曰,wang'zi'qing'ji'jian'er'wen'yan'yue
王子搜不肯出,wang'zi'sou'bu'ken'chu
王子搜非恶为君也,wang'zi'sou'fei'e'wei'jun'ye
王子搜患之,wang'zi'sou'huan'zhi
忘足,wang'zu
妄作孝弟,wang'zuo'xiao'di
未败墨子道,wei'bai'mo'zi'dao
为崩为蹶,wei'beng'wei'jue
未必贵也,wei'bi'gui'ye
未必贱也,wei'bi'jian'ye
未必为其服也,wei'bi'wei'qi'fu'ye
未必知其道也,wei'bi'zhi'qi'dao'ye
为不善乎显明之中者,wei'bu'shan'hu'xian'ming'zhi'zhong'zhe
唯不饮酒,wei'bu'yin'jiu
未尝不荒也,wei'chang'bu'huang'ye
未尝不始于是之,wei'chang'bu'shi'yu'shi'zhi
未尝不言,wei'chang'bu'yan
未尝得闻此言也,wei'chang'de'wen'ci'yan'ye
未尝敢以耗气也,wei'chang'gan'yi'hao'qi'ye
未尝敢饮食君之酒肉,wei'chang'gan'yin'shi'jun'zhi'jiu'rou
未尝好田而鹑生于夭,wei'chang'hao'tian'er'chun'sheng'yu'yao
未尝见材如此其美也,wei'chang'jian'cai'ru'ci'qi'mei'ye
未尝见夫子遇人如此其威也,wei'chang'jian'fu'zi'yu'ren'ru'ci'qi'wei'ye
未尝见全牛也,wei'chang'jian'quan'niu'ye
未尝绝音,wei'chang'jue'yin
未尝先人而常随人,wei'chang'xian'ren'er'chang'sui'ren
未尝言,wei'chang'yan
未尝有闻其唱者也,wei'chang'you'wen'qi'chang'zhe'ye
未尝有罪,wei'chang'you'zui

未达人心,wei'da'ren'xin

维斗得之,wei'dou'de'zhi

谓伐与不伐乱人也者,wei'fa'yu'bu'fa'luan'ren'ye'zhe
微夫子之发吾覆也,wei'fu'zi'zhi'fa'wu'fu'ye
威公曰,wei'gong'yue
唯贾人也,wei'gu'ren'ye
为后世虑,wei'hou'shi'lv
位乎得,wei'hu'de
谓己道人,wei'ji'dao'ren
未既其实,wei'ji'qi'shi
谓己谀人,wei'ji'yu'ren
唯剑士也,wei'jian'shi'ye
唯简之而不得,wei'jian'zhi'er'bu'de
未解裙襦,wei'jie'qun'ru

为君攻之,wei'jun'gong'zhi
唯君所病之何也,wei'jun'suo'bing'zhi'he'ye
为亢而已矣,wei'kang'er'yi'yi
未可以为常也,wei'ke'yi'wei'chang'ye
未可知也,wei'ke'zhi'ye
唯恐缄滕扃谲之不固也,wei'kong'jian'teng'jiong'jue'zhi'bu'gu'ye
唯恐其不受也,wei'kong'qi'bu'shou'ye
畏垒大壤,wei'lei'da'rang

未离其内,wei'li'qi'nei

尾闾泄之,wei'lv'xie'zhi
未免于物而终以为过,wei'mian'yu'wu'er'zhong'yi'wei'guo
慰愍沈屯,wei'min'shen'tun
唯命之从,wei'ming'zhi'cong
魏牟,wei'mou
为内刑者,wei'nei'xing'zhe
为能与人相将迎,wei'neng'yu'ren'xiang'jiang'ying
未能自胜也,wei'neng'zi'sheng'ye
为圃者忿然作色而笑曰,wei'pu'zhe'fen'ran'zuo'se'er'xiao'yue
为圃者仰而视之曰,wei'pu'zhe'yang'er'shi'zhi'yue
为圃者曰,wei'pu'zhe'yue
谓其不亏其神也,wei'qi'bu'kui'qi'shen'ye
为其布与,wei'qi'bu'yu
为其服者,wei'qi'fu'zhe
为其贵非其贵也,wei'qi'gui'fei'qi'gui'ye
唯其好之,wei'qi'hao'zhi

谓其无以益其乐而已矣,wei'qi'wu'yi'yi'qi'le'er'yi'yi
唯且无诚,wei'qie'wu'cheng
唯全人能之,wei'quan'ren'neng'zhi

魏然而已矣,wei'ran'er'yi'yi
